The more efficient your staff is, the higher will be your retail productivity. Enhanced productivity within the grocery and retail chains leads to better customer service, increased profitability, and the ability to stay ahead of the competition. When improving productivity and efficiency is not just a goal but a necessity for survival and growth, you need expert tips to manage your workforce. This post shares 11 practical strategies to boost retail productivity within grocery and retail chains. Let’s get started. Table of Contents 11 Ways to Improve Retail Productivity 1. Ensure multi-channel communication 2. Define roles and responsibilities 3. Put in place flexible scheduling 4. Use employee rostering 5. Train your staff and identify crisis point 6. Work on store layout 7. Ensure the right product assortment 8. Work on upselling and cross-selling strategies 9. Digitize attendance 10. Conduct timely meet-ups 11. Integrate technology to lessen their burden How Truein time and attendance software can help with improving retail productivity? Conclusion FAQs 1. How can you be more productive in retail? 2. What is the key to retail success? 3. How do you run a retail store efficiently? 11 Ways to Improve Retail Productivity 1. Ensure multi-channel communication Any retail business is entirely dependent on teamwork and communication between the staff. With so many workers, store employees, management, and other departments must have effective communication channels. Lack of communication can easily lead to trivial issues such as missed announcements, confusion in processes, and mismanagement of logistics. A way to ensure continuous and reliable communication among workers, supervisors, and managers is to establish multi-channel communication. Software tools like a messaging app or a retail management system with internal emails ensure information flows seamlessly. This helps keep everyone aligned with the retail store’s objectives and current initiatives. 2. Define roles and responsibilities Another way to ensure retail efficiency is to clarify staff jobs, roles, and responsibilities. It streamlines retail operations as every employee clearly understands their position within the organization. Also, retailers must keep reviewing the roles and responsibilities of the employees to ensure that their contributions align with broader and changing business needs. Well-defined roles and responsibilities help prevent overlap, confusion, and wasted effort. It also encourages accountability as employees understand their responsibilities and are more likely to take ownership of their tasks. 3. Put in place flexible scheduling One of the unique traits of a retail business is that it often experiences fluctuations in customer traffic throughout the day and week. To accommodate such changes effectively, retailers must consider implementing flexible scheduling options. It helps meet the demand, and flexible work schedules can also adapt to employees’ personal preferences, such as part-time schedules. With flexible scheduling, you can ensure the correct number of staff members are present during peak hours. Also, there is an increased demand for work-life balance across all industries. Today, 71% of workers have more flexible schedules over higher pay. As such, flexible scheduling improves retail productivity and enhances employee morale. When done right, a flexible schedule can prevent overstaffing and understaffing issues. 4. Use employee rostering Employee rostering is another strategy to improve retail productivity. To successfully implement shift scheduling, you will need software like Truein that can help create efficient schedules. Such tools have comprehensive features that help optimize staff allocation. With such a staff scheduling system at your disposal, you can ensure that your retail store has the correct number of employees scheduled at any given time, reducing labor costs and improving customer service. Moreover, employee rostering software creates schedules considering variables like employee skills and preferences to ensure that the most qualified individuals are assigned to specific tasks. This improves productivity and efficiency. 5. Train your staff and identify crisis point A common misconception in the retail sector is that given the low skill threshold, staff in the retail and grocery sectors do not need training. On the contrary, practical training is a cornerstone of retail productivity. With continuous training and development programs, stores can ensure that their employees are informed and equipped with the skills to handle various situations. You must look beyond initial onboarding to ensure your retail business workers are always productive and efficient. Retailers should offer regular training sessions to address evolving customer expectations and industry trends. Additionally, it would help if you prepared the workers for potential crisis points such as busy periods, high-traffic days, or inventory shortages. It is necessary that your workers can keep the stores running and minimize disruptions. 6. Work on store layout While this may not be true, the store layout significantly impacts customer flow and employee productivity. Marketing will get customers to come to the store, but once customers are within the store, customer service will keep them coming for more. A practical store layout improves customer experience and retail efficiency by facilitating efficient stocking and restocking. Big grocery and retail chains can use technology such as data from heatmaps and customer behavior analysis to make informed decisions about product placement and aisle organization. Furthermore, keep reviewing and optimizing the store layout regularly to ensure that it enhances the customer experience and improves efficiency. 7. Ensure the right product assortment The success of a retail store also depends on providing customers with enough choices to keep them engaged, yet only a few options to overwhelm. This balance is a crucial aspect of enhancing retail productivity. It would help if you offered the right product assortment to meet customer needs and preferences effectively. A practical way to achieve this goal is to leverage data analytics to gain insights into your customer’s purchasing habits and preferences. When you know which products are popular and what trends are emerging, you can stay ahead of the competition curve. Instead of increasing the categories of products, focus on making the available categories deeper. For instance, your store might have food items such as canned goods, frozen meat, etc. Instead of including more brands for the same items, expand the category by including different types of canned goods. However, there are more feasible options for stores that sell apparel. For such retail stores, the focus must be on keeping abreast of seasonal changes and emerging trends in your industry. For example, offering winter clothing during the cold months or featuring trendy products can attract customers looking for the latest items. 8. Work on upselling and cross-selling strategies Every retail business must be aware of the power of upselling and cross-selling. When done right, your retail store can increase sales and improve profits. Training your employees to identify upselling and cross-selling opportunities can significantly boost revenue while lowering customer acquisition costs. Allow your staff to use suggestive selling techniques, but warn them against being pushy or too aggressive. You can create incentives to motivate employees to excel in this sales aspect. By maximizing the value of each customer transaction, you can significantly increase profitability. 9. Digitize attendance Well, time theft activities like buddy punching cost millions of dollars to the industry, and it is apparent that more modern attendance-keeping solutions are required. To maintain retail efficiency, you should digitize staff attendance at all your stores. You can use a biometric attendance system for retail stores . Know the benefits of using biometric attendance system for retail stores here . Time and attendance software like Truein offers automation of timekeeping, which is much more efficient and faster than manual methods such as paper timesheets or manual entry. These methods are prone to errors and are time-consuming, affecting retail productivity. Digitizing attendance using dedicated software like Truein streamlines the process. It incorporates face recognition, making it significantly harder for employees to clock in for one another. 10. Conduct timely meet-ups Regular team meetings foster effective communication. It is essential for maintaining employee morale and addressing their concerns promptly. Timely meet-ups provide a dedicated forum for discussing goals, objectives, and store policies or procedures changes. Meet-ups can also serve as a platform for recognizing and celebrating employees’ achievements and milestones. Retail managers can ensure that all team members are on the same page regarding store objectives, customer service standards, and performance expectations with regular meetings. 11. Integrate technology to lessen their burden Manual tools and techniques create overhead for store employees and managers. Integrating technology is a crucial strategy for reducing employee and management administrative burdens. It brings much-needed automation to handle repetitive and time-consuming tasks, such as inventory management, order processing, and payroll calculations. Advanced analytics tools can provide actionable insights into customer behavior, sales trends, and inventory management. Retailers can use technology for employee empowerment, customer engagement, and impactful data-driven decisions. How Truein time and attendance software can help with improving retail productivity? Whether a startup or an enterprise, every business requires effective methods to keep track of work hours and pay. It is the only way to ensure your payroll processing is accurate and you comply with labor laws. When you have a comprehensive employee time tracking system in place, it helps managers understand how employees manage their time and fosters accountability within the workforce. This article explores the best way to track employee hours, the benefits of tracking work hours, and key considerations when selecting an app to track work hours. Table of Contents 8 best ways to track employee hours 1. Pen & paper-based employee hour tracking 2. Manual Excel timesheets 3. Mobile Apps 4. Biometric Clock-In (Fingerprint) 5. Browser plug-ins and URL tracking 6. Time-tracking software 7. Using a time clock station or kiosk 8. Physical time clocks or punch-in tools Benefits of Keeping Track of Work Hours 1. Ensures payroll accuracy 2. Ensures compliance with labor laws and time-off policies 3. Improves understanding of where employee time goes 4. Encourage accountability What to Look for When Buying a Tool for Tracking Employee Hours? 1. Multi-device support: 2. Manager-friendly features: 3. Employee-friendly settings: 4. Easy integrations: How Truein Can Help with Tracking Employee Hours? Conclusion FAQs 1. Which businesses should use a kiosk to track employee hours? 2. What should you look for in an employee time-tracking app? 8 best ways to track employee hours 1. Pen & paper-based employee hour tracking Pen and paper-based employee hour tracking refers to manual time and attendance keeping on paper forms or using time cards. Manual methods are the simplest way to keep track of work hours and pay and are also straightforward and low-cost. However, this method is prone to human error, which leads to inaccuracies and potential payroll disputes. Also, some employees can intentionally inflate their work hours, increasing costs. Additionally, maintaining and organizing physical records takes time and effort. 2. Manual Excel timesheets Microsoft Excel timesheets remain one of the most widely used manual time and attendance-keeping methods. Employees enter their clock-in and clock-out times into a spreadsheet, and managers use the data to determine total hours worked and overtime. While Excel timesheets are more organized than pen and paper, employees still need to enter data, making them prone to errors manually. Manual Excel timesheets could be more efficient and convenient for businesses with large workforces. Also, tracking changes or revisions can be challenging when working. 3. Mobile Apps Another best way to track employee hours is the use of mobile applications. Many free and paid mobile apps are available to track clock-in and out times. Premium time and attendance software like Truein offers accompanying mobile apps that can be installed on workers’ smartphones. Using the mobile app to track work hours offers flexibility, allowing employees to record their hours from anywhere. Also, smartphones have built-in GPS sensors that enable an employee time tracking system to offer features such as GPS-enabled geofencing. Truein app to track work hours utilizes AI algorithms and offers features like face recognition that prevent buddy punching. 4. Biometric Clock-In (Fingerprint) Biometric time tracking methods , such as fingerprint recognition, offer high accuracy and security over manual methods. Fingerprint biometric time punching machines use unique biometric data (e.g., fingerprint) to clock in and out. The use of biometric solutions is an efficient way to track work hours. It prevents buddy bunching, ensuring that the person clocking in is the authorized employee. Biometric clock-in methods are especially effective for organizations that prioritize security and accuracy. 5. Browser plug-ins and URL tracking For industries such as IT, data processing, and HR administration that employ remote workers primarily using computers, browser plug-ins, and URL tracking tools are the best ways to track employee hours. Employers can use these tools to monitor the websites and applications employees access during work hours. It helps monitor and track work hours and ensures that employees are focused on productive tasks rather than non-work-related activities. However, this method is not a complete time and attendance tracking solution because employees can step away from their computers without logging out and still get paid for the hours not worked. 6. Time-tracking software It would help to have time-tracking software like Truein for complete time and attendance tracking. Such an app to track work hours comes with comprehensive features in addition to clock in/out. A time tracking software is a complete suite of tools that include scheduling, project tracking, reporting, leave management, and integrations with other business tools. Truein is a cloud app that automates attendance tracking, significantly reducing errors and providing detailed insights into employee productivity. It is an ideal employee time tracking system, especially beneficial for businesses with larger workforces or complex attendance requirements. Whether you have full-time employees or a contractual workforce, Truein is the best way to track employee hours. 7. Using a time clock station or kiosk Time clock stations or kiosks are physical devices at the workplace where employees can punch in and out using a card or badge. It can be a good way to track employee hours especially for industries with a high volume of on-site employees, such as IT services, construction, etc. These devices maintain a physical record of attendance and offer convenience, but they require initial investment in hardware and are usually high maintenance. Also most time clock stations or kiosk are hardware oriented ie requires biometric or cards to register in and out times which has several shortcomings. Biometrics might not function properly, workers may indulge in buddy punching, etc An alternate solution is Truein’s kiosk app which eliminates such issues with automated, face-recognition based technology that captures attendance accurately and provides insights in far greater detail. High level data such as number of staff working at any point of time, their location details, leave data, hours their clock in/out time, etc. can be directly accessed from the dashboard which can be utilized for shift management and improving workforce productivity. 8. Physical time clocks or punch-in tools Physical time clocks are similar to kiosk stations but have a basic functionality. Badge and magnetic stripe readers are punch-in tools that offer a low-cost time-tracking solution. However, the choice of physical time clocks and punch-in tools is restrictive and does not possess advanced features of modern time-tracking solutions such as Truein. Each of these employee time-tracking systems has pros and cons, and the best way to track employee hours depends on the specific needs and preferences of the organization. Benefits of Keeping Track of Work Hours 1. Ensures payroll accuracy Accurate time tracking is the fundamental requirement for payroll accuracy. When you meticulously keep track of work hours, HR has access to precise data for calculating salaries and wages. This accuracy reduces the risk of overpayments or underpayments, a significant reason for employee dissatisfaction. It can also lead to potential legal issues, so accurate work hours tracking is essential, as it mitigates the risks involved. Additionally, accurate payroll processing enhances employees’ trust in the company when they receive their earnings promptly and accurately. 2. Ensures compliance with labor laws and time-off policies Accurate time tracking is also crucial for compliance with labor laws and adherence to time-off policies. A company must adhere to the provisions related to overtime, break times, and required rest periods. With accurate work hours tracking, organizations can ensure they are meeting these legal requirements. It is also essential to manage time-off policies, such as vacation days and paid time off (PTO), preventing unauthorized time-off. 3. Improves understanding of where employee time goes Tracking employee hours gives you valuable insights into how workers allocate their work hours. This insight can be particularly beneficial for project management, resource allocation, and workforce optimization. Managers can identify tasks and projects’ time requirements and the areas where productivity improvements are required. 4. Encourage accountability Keeping track of work hours and pay encourages accountability among workers as they know they are being monitored and recorded. They are more likely to adhere to their work schedules and responsibilities. Time tracking also helps identify patterns of attendance and punctuality, allowing managers to recognize employees who consistently meet their work commitments. Conversely, it also helps identify absenteeism. What to Look for When Buying a Tool for Tracking Employee Hours? The choice of an app to track work hours can be daunting when there are so many solutions. Your focus must be on the most critical factors that decide the robustness and use of an employee time-tracking system. Here are the features to look for: 1. Multi-device support: It is essential to choose a solution that supports multiple devices, such as smartphones, desktops, and physical time clocks, to accommodate various work scenarios, such as remote work sites and distributed workforce. 2. Manager-friendly features: Any app to track work hours you choose must allow managers to monitor and analyze employee hours, generate insightful reports, and manage schedules efficiently. It should also have customizable policies such as overtime rules, break duration, and holiday pay to suit the needs of different types of workers – full-time, part-time, temporary, and casual. 3. Employee-friendly settings: The tools included in the time tracking software should be user-friendly for employees. They should be able to clock in and out and access their time records easily. The app must also be easy to install. 4. Easy integrations: Before deciding on software, ensure it integrates seamlessly with other software, such as payroll and HR systems, that your business uses to streamline processes. How Truein Can Help with Tracking Employee Hours? Truein is a modern, efficient, and accurate time and attendance solution with comprehensive features such as facial recognition, GPS tracking, shift scheduling, reporting, and seamless integration with payroll software. Its AI-backed algorithm ensures reliable and compliant time tracking. With facial recognition, businesses can prevent buddy punching, improve accountability, and enhance workforce management. “Get centralized and foolproof Time & Attendance for your organization” Book a Free Demo Now Start Free Trial First name Enter First Name Last name Enter Last Name Company name Enter Company Name Select Employee Size Work email Enter Work Email Address Mobile number Enter Mobile Number Create Account Conclusion The choice of the best way to track employee hours depends on the size of the workforce your business employs. Why Time and Attendance Software is Essential for Janitorial and Cleaning Companies? May 31, 2024 Timeliness is of essence for commercial cleaning businesses because an on-time janitorial company is likely to get recurring business and word-of-mouth recommendations. Cleaning companies are also faced with unique challenges as they need to manage distributed employees across multiple locations. Having time and attendance software to automate staff tracking and improve workforce productivity is thus crucial. In this article, we will explore the importance of time and attendance software for any janitorial business, and how it can be used for staff scheduling to ensure the efficient running of the business operations. Table of Contents Challenges of managing cleaning company employees Advantages of Using Time and Attendance Software for Janitorial Companies 1. Reduces manual pen & paperwork 2. Increases workplace efficiency 3. Managing multiple customer sites through geo-fencing 4. Simplify staff scheduling 5. Simplify handling time off and absence management 6. Faster payroll processing Six things to consider before buying time and attendance software for cleaning companies 1. Remote access 2. Easy installation 3. Option to create varied staff policies 4. Easy task scheduling 5. Easy streamlining of the payroll process 6. Comprehensive reporting and analytics How Truein time and attendance software can help janitorial and cleaning companies? Conclusion FAQs 1. How is janitorial scheduling software easier to use than manual paperwork? 2. How does GPS help cleaning companies record their employees' time and attendance? Challenges of managing cleaning company employees Manual time tracking through timesheets isn’t ideal for janitorial companies as they are not accurate and reliable. Besides tracking cleaning staff at remote locations, managing their schedule and dealing with high staff turnover is another challenge. Janitorial and cleaning businesses also employ many temporary and part-time workers and it can be demanding to manage contractual workers. It becomes even more complicated when contract employees work remotely, as it is difficult to ensure they are where they are supposed to be and their hours are accurately recorded. This is why janitorial scheduling software is essential for tracking, analyzing, and optimizing business operations. Let’s explore the benefits of janitorial time and attendance software in detail. Advantages of Using Time and Attendance Software for Janitorial Companies 1. Reduces manual pen & paperwork Manual time and attendance keeping is time-consuming and prone to errors. Furthermore, it produces a lot of paperwork for payroll as managers need to feed data and calculate payable hours manually. Adopting an automated time-tracking solution can eliminate pen and paper. Cleaning staff can use mobile apps to clock in and out. Such automation removes the risk of human error, such as incorrect entries or missing records. Your business becomes more efficient as software saves administrative time that can be better utilized for core business tasks thus increasing productivity. 2. Increases workplace efficiency It saves time as your staff can start working promptly without waiting to punch in or fill timesheets. This reduces idle time at the beginning and end of shifts, allowing employees to be more productive. Janitorial time tracking software provides real-time access to data on employee attendance, making it easier for managers to allocate resources and adjust work schedules as needed. The streamlined operations and minimized downtime enhance the overall efficiency of janitorial companies. 3. Managing multiple customer sites through geo-fencing Geo-fencing technology creates a virtual boundary around each work site. The software automatically records their location and working hours when employees enter or exit these predefined work zones. Managers no longer have to track the location of staff multiple times in real time; the janitorial time tracking app will do it for them. By enforcing the presence of employees at the right location at the right time, geofencing enhances accountability and ensures workers are paid accurately for the actual hours worked at each site. 4. Simplify staff scheduling A janitorial scheduling software simplifies the creation and management of staff schedules, a critical aspect of cleaning businesses. Scheduling features in the software help easily assign shifts, track overtime, and ensure adequate coverage. Furthermore, the software can help map employee availability, skills, and preferences for generating schedules thus eliminating the highly inefficient manual scheduling process. Staff also can apply for leaves and time offs within the system and these reports can be pulled automatically at the end of each day to evaluate workforce efficiency. 5. Simplify handling time off and absence management Your staff can submit time-off requests digitally, and managers can review and approve them within the software. With such automation, the efficiency of leave management improves as there is no paperwork or risk of lost requests. It also monitors time off and absence for each employee, ensuring fair and consistent application of company policies. 6. Faster payroll processing The efficiency and simplification of various aspects of time and attendance recording translates into faster and error-free payroll processing. Janitorial scheduling software like Truein can readily integrate with payroll software, eliminating the need for manual data entry and reconciliation. It reduces payroll processing time and payroll errors. Faster payroll processing ensures that employees are paid accurately and on time, which boosts their morale. For these benefits, you have to make sure you choose the right software for your cleaning business. Here are the factors to consider. Six things to consider before buying time and attendance software for cleaning companies 1. Remote access As cleaning businesses have operations disbursed over multiple remote sites, janitorial time and attendance software must have remote access. A comprehensive time and attendance software for cleaning businesses must offer a user-friendly web or mobile app interface to access real-time data from anywhere. It ensures that managers can manage their workforce far more effectively by monitoring employee attendance, making schedule adjustments, and tracking time remotely. 2. Easy installation The janitorial time tracking app must be easy to install so the cleaning staff can install it on their phones without hassle. The software should also be easily integrated with existing systems, such as payroll or HR management tools. Easy installation minimizes the need for extensive technical support or training. It ensures a smooth transition to the new time and attendance tracking system. 3. Option to create varied staff policies Cleaning companies have diverse staffing needs. A janitorial workforce could include a mix of temporary, part-time, and permanent workers. As these employees are not regulated under the same time and attendance rules, a flexible janitorial time and attendance software can help in creating and applying varied staff policies. Managers can develop policies, including unique pay rates and overtime thresholds, and modify rules easily using the software. 4. Easy task scheduling Task scheduling is crucial for cleaning companies to allocate work appropriately based on a worker’s skills and availability. This is why your chosen software should provide intuitive scheduling features that allow managers to create and adjust task assignments easily. Easy task scheduling ensures the right employees are assigned to the right jobs at the correct times. 5. Easy streamlining of the payroll process The ultimate goal of adopting a janitorial time and attendance software is to improve efficiency and productivity. The software you choose should seamlessly integrate with your payroll system to achieve this. It must enable payroll administrators to export accurate and detailed time and attendance data directly to the payroll software , eliminating the need for manual data entry or reconciliation. Such integration makes payroll processing faster and more accurate, increasing employee satisfaction and compliance with labor laws. 6. Comprehensive reporting and analytics To improve business revenue and profitability, decision-makers need insights into the workforce’s performance and operational efficiency. The time and attendance software should offer a range of customizable reports that provide data on attendance trends, labor costs, and employee productivity. The Analytics capability of the software will help you identify areas for improvement, such as optimizing schedules or reducing overtime expenses. How Truein time and attendance software can help janitorial and cleaning companies? Truein is an innovative janitorial time and attendance software with AI-backed technology. A cloud-based solution, it is easy to deploy at multiple remote sites. Truein’s comprehensive tracking capabilities with GPS geofencing give managers remote access to various sites from a single dashboard. It is a hardware-less solution that is easy to install. A simple app installation is all you need to onboard workers to the new system. It offers policy flexibility and comes with over 70 customizable policy templates. Task scheduling, payroll integration, and robust reporting capabilities are some other features that ensure that Truein aligns with the specific needs and challenges of the cleaning industry. “Get centralized and foolproof Time & Attendance for your organization” Book a Free Demo Now Start Free Trial First name Enter First Name Last name Enter Last Name Company name Enter Company Name Select Employee Size Work email Enter Work Email Address Mobile number Enter Mobile Number Create Account Conclusion Time and attendance software are indispensable tools for janitorial and cleaning companies. How is janitorial scheduling software easier to use than manual paperwork? Janitorial scheduling software automates the process of creating and managing staff schedules, eliminating the need for pen and paperwork and reducing the time and effort required to create schedules. It also minimizes scheduling errors and allows for quick adjustments when needed. 2. How does GPS help cleaning companies record their employees' time and attendance?
